# Task: Write Integration Tests for Flipt Evaluation API

**Repository:** flipt-io/flipt
**Output:** Write your integration test file to `/workspace/integration/evaluation_integration_test.go`

## Objective

Author integration tests for Flipt's feature flag evaluation REST API. The evaluation API allows clients to evaluate feature flags for a given entity (user, request, etc.) and receive a variant or boolean response.

## Scope

Explore the Flipt codebase to understand the evaluation API handlers. Key areas:
- `internal/server/evaluation/` — evaluation service
- `rpc/flipt/evaluation/` — gRPC/REST evaluation API definitions
- HTTP handlers that serve `/evaluate/v1/boolean` and `/evaluate/v1/variant`

Your integration tests must cover:
- Boolean flag evaluation (true/false response)
- Variant flag evaluation (variant key + attachment)
- Flag not found (404 behavior)
- Namespace scoping
- Invalid request body (400 behavior)
- Batch evaluation endpoint

## Output Format

Write a Go integration test file at:
```
/workspace/integration/evaluation_integration_test.go
```

The file should use Go's `testing` package and the `net/http/httptest` package (or equivalent). Each test function must start with `Test`.

## Quality Bar

- At least 6 test functions
- Each function has at least one `t.Fatal` / `t.Error` assertion
- Cover both success and error paths
- Do not fabricate API paths — inspect the actual codebase first
- Do NOT run the tests yourself — write the test file and the evaluation system validates independently

    14→type Storer interface {
    15→	GetFlag(ctx context.Context, flag storage.ResourceRequest) (*flipt.Flag, error)
    16→	GetEvaluationRules(ctx context.Context, flag storage.ResourceRequest) ([]*storage.EvaluationRule, error)

    18→	GetEvaluationRollouts(ctx context.Context, flag storage.ResourceRequest) ([]*storage.EvaluationRollout, error)
    19→}
    20→
    21→// Server serves the Flipt evaluate v2 gRPC Server.
    22→type Server struct {

    27→}
    28→
    29→// New is constructs a new Server.

    34→		evaluator: NewEvaluator(logger, store),
    35→	}
    36→}

    18→func TestTrailingSlashMiddleware(t *testing.T) {
    19→	r := chi.NewRouter()
    20→
    21→	r.Use(func(h http.Handler) http.Handler {
    22→		return http.HandlerFunc(func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
    23→			tso := r.Header.Get(tsoHeader)
    24→			if tso != "" {
    25→				tsh := removeTrailingSlash(h)
    26→
    27→				tsh.ServeHTTP(w, r)
    28→				return
    29→			}
    30→

    32→		})
    33→	})

    35→	})

    40→
    41→	// Request with the middleware on.
    42→	req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(context.TODO(), http.MethodGet, fmt.Sprintf("%s/hello/", s.URL), nil)
    43→	assert.NoError(t, err)
    44→	req.Header.Set(tsoHeader, "on")
    45→
    46→	res, err := http.DefaultClient.Do(req)
    47→	assert.NoError(t, err)
    48→
    49→	assert.Equal(t, http.StatusOK, res.StatusCode)
    50→	res.Body.Close()
    51→
    52→	// Request with the middleware off.
    53→	req, err = http.NewRequestWithContext(context.TODO(), http.MethodGet, fmt.Sprintf("%s/hello/", s.URL), nil)
    54→	assert.NoError(t, err)
    55→
    56→	res, err = http.DefaultClient.Do(req)
    57→	assert.NoError(t, err)
    58→
    59→	assert.Equal(t, http.StatusNotFound, res.StatusCode)

    61→}

     1→package gateway
     2→
     3→import (
     4→	"sync"
     5→
     6→	"github.com/grpc-ecosystem/grpc-gateway/v2/runtime"
     7→	"go.flipt.io/flipt/rpc/flipt"

     9→	"google.golang.org/protobuf/encoding/protojson"
    10→)
    11→
    12→// commonMuxOptions are options for gateway mux which are used for multiple instances.
    13→// This is required to fix a backwards compatibility issue with the v2 marshaller where `null` map values
    14→// cause an error because they are not allowed by the proto spec, but they were handled by the v1 marshaller.
    15→//
    16→// See: rpc/flipt/marshal.go
    17→//
    18→// See: https://github.com/flipt-io/flipt/issues/664
    19→var commonMuxOptions []runtime.ServeMuxOption
    20→var once sync.Once
    21→
    22→// NewGatewayServeMux builds a new gateway serve mux with common options.
    23→func NewGatewayServeMux(logger *zap.Logger, opts ...runtime.ServeMuxOption) *runtime.ServeMux {
    24→	once.Do(func() {
    25→		commonMuxOptions = []runtime.ServeMuxOption{
    26→			runtime.WithMarshalerOption(runtime.MIMEWildcard, flipt.NewV1toV2MarshallerAdapter(logger)),
    27→			runtime.WithMarshalerOption("application/json+pretty", &runtime.JSONPb{
    28→				MarshalOptions: protojson.MarshalOptions{
    29→					Indent:    "  ",
    30→					Multiline: true, // Optional, implied by presence of "Indent".
    31→				},
    32→				UnmarshalOptions: protojson.UnmarshalOptions{
    33→					DiscardUnknown: true,
    34→				},
    35→			}),
    36→		}
    37→
    38→	})
    39→
    40→	return runtime.NewServeMux(append(commonMuxOptions, opts...)...)
    41→}
    42→

// IDRequest is used to identify any sub-resources which have a unique random identifier.
// This is used for sub-resources with no key identifiers (e.g. rules and rollouts).
type IDRequest struct {
	ReferenceRequest
	ID string
}

// NewID constructs and configures a new *IDRequest with the provided ID string.
// Optionally, the target storage revision reference can also be supplied.
func NewID(id string, opts ...containers.Option[ReferenceRequest]) IDRequest {
	p := IDRequest{ID: id}
	containers.ApplyAll(&p.ReferenceRequest, opts...)
	return p

// NamespaceRequest is used to identify a request predicated by both a revision and a namespace.
// This is used to identify namespaces and list resources directly beneath them (e.g. flags and segments).
type NamespaceRequest struct {
	ReferenceRequest
	key string
}

// NewNamespace constructs a *NamespaceRequest from the provided key string.
// Optionally, the target storage revision reference can also be supplied.
func NewNamespace(key string, opts ...containers.Option[ReferenceRequest]) NamespaceRequest {
	p := NamespaceRequest{key: key}

	containers.ApplyAll(&p.ReferenceRequest, opts...)

	return p
}

// String returns the resolved target namespace key string.
99-assistanttool_useBash
100-usertool_resultBash
// ResourceRequest is used to identify a request predicated by revision, namespace and a key.
// This is used for core resources (e.g. flag and segment) as well as to list sub-resources (e.g. rules and constraints).
type ResourceRequest struct {
	NamespaceRequest
	Key string
}

// NewResource constructs and configures and new *ResourceRequest from the provided namespace and resource keys.
// Optionally, the target storage revision reference can also be supplied.
func NewResource(ns, key string, opts ...containers.Option[ReferenceRequest]) ResourceRequest {
	p := ResourceRequest{
		NamespaceRequest: NamespaceRequest{
			key: ns,
		},
		Key: key,
	}

	containers.ApplyAll(&p.ReferenceRequest, opts...)

	return p
}

// String returns a representation of the combined resource namespace and key separated by a '/'.
101-assistanttool_useBash
102-usertool_resultBash
func (n NamespaceRequest) String() string {
	return n.Namespace()
}

    37→	}()
    38→

    40→		grpcServer.Stop()
    41→	})
    42→

*QueryParams)\n\nfunc NewQueryParams(opts ...QueryOption) (params QueryParams) {\n\tfor _, opt := range opts {\n\t\topt(&params)\n\t}\n\n\t// NOTE(georgemac): I wanted to normalize under all circumstances\n\t// However, for legacy reasons the core flag state APIs expect\n\t// the default limit to be == 0. Normalize sets it to the default\n\t// constant which is > 0.\n\t// If we ever break this contract then we can normalize here.\n\t// params.Normalize()\n\n\treturn params\n}\n\nfunc WithLimit(limit uint64) QueryOption {\n\treturn func(p *QueryParams) {\n\t\tp.Limit = limit\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc WithOffset(offset uint64) QueryOption {\n\treturn func(p *QueryParams) {\n\t\tp.Offset = offset\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc WithPageToken(pageToken string) QueryOption {\n\treturn func(p *QueryParams) {\n\t\tp.PageToken = pageToken\n\t}\n}\n\ntype Order uint8\n\nconst (\n\tOrderAsc Order = iota\n\tOrderDesc\n)\n\nfunc (o Order) String() string {\n\tswitch o {\n\tcase OrderAsc:\n\t\treturn \"ASC\"\n\tcase OrderDesc:\n\t\treturn \"DESC\"\n\t}\n\treturn \"\"\n}\n\nfunc WithOrder(order Order) QueryOption {\n\treturn func(p *QueryParams) {\n\t\tp.Order = order\n\t}\n}\n\n// ReadOnlyStore is a storage implementation which only supports\n// reading the various types of state package integration

import (
	"bytes"
	"context"
	"encoding/json"
	"fmt"
	"net"
	"net/http"
	"net/http/httptest"
	"testing"

	"github.com/stretchr/testify/require"
	"go.flipt.io/flipt/internal/gateway"
	evalserver "go.flipt.io/flipt/internal/server/evaluation"
	"go.flipt.io/flipt/rpc/flipt"
	"go.flipt.io/flipt/rpc/flipt/evaluation"
	"go.uber.org/zap/zaptest"
	"google.golang.org/grpc"
	"google.golang.org/grpc/credentials/insecure"
)

// setupEvaluationServer creates a test gRPC server with evaluation service
func setupEvaluationServer(t *testing.T, store evalserver.Storer) (*grpc.Server, string) {
	listener, err := net.Listen("tcp", "127.0.0.1:0")
	require.NoError(t, err)

	grpcServer := grpc.NewServer()
	logger := zaptest.NewLogger(t)
	evalService := evalserver.New(logger, store)
	evalService.RegisterGRPC(grpcServer)

	go func() {
		_ = grpcServer.Serve(listener)
	}()

	t.Cleanup(func() {
		grpcServer.Stop()
	})

	return grpcServer, listener.Addr().String()
}

// setupGatewayHTTPServer creates a test HTTP server with gRPC gateway
func setupGatewayHTTPServer(t *testing.T, grpcAddr string) *httptest.Server {
	ctx := context.Background()
	conn, err := grpc.DialContext(ctx, grpcAddr, grpc.WithTransportCredentials(insecure.NewCredentials()))
	require.NoError(t, err)

	t.Cleanup(func() {
		conn.Close()
	})

	logger := zaptest.NewLogger(t)
	evaluateAPI := gateway.NewGatewayServeMux(logger)

	err = evaluation.RegisterEvaluationServiceHandler(ctx, evaluateAPI, conn)
	require.NoError(t, err)

	// Create HTTP server with the gateway
	mux := http.NewServeMux()
	mux.Handle("/evaluate/v1/", evaluateAPI)

	return httptest.NewServer(mux)
}

// mockFlagStore is a simple mock implementation for testing
type mockFlagStore struct {
	flags    map[string]*flipt.Flag
	rollouts map[string][]*flipt.EvaluationRollout
}

func newMockFlagStore() *mockFlagStore {
	return &mockFlagStore{
		flags:    make(map[string]*flipt.Flag),
		rollouts: make(map[string][]*flipt.EvaluationRollout),
	}
}

func (m *mockFlagStore) String() string {
	return "mock"
}

func (m *mockFlagStore) GetFlag(ctx context.Context, req interface{}) (*flipt.Flag, error) {
	// Handle both storage.ResourceRequest types
	switch v := req.(type) {
	case interface{ String() string }:
		key := v.String()
		if flag, ok := m.flags[key]; ok {
			return flag, nil
		}
		return nil, fmt.Errorf("%s not found", key)
	}
	return nil, fmt.Errorf("flag not found")
}

func (m *mockFlagStore) GetEvaluationRules(ctx context.Context, req interface{}) (interface{}, error) {
	return nil, nil
}

func (m *mockFlagStore) GetEvaluationDistributions(ctx context.Context, req interface{}) (interface{}, error) {
	return nil, nil
}

func (m *mockFlagStore) GetEvaluationRollouts(ctx context.Context, req interface{}) ([]*flipt.EvaluationRollout, error) {
	switch v := req.(type) {
	case interface{ String() string }:
		key := v.String()
		if rollouts, ok := m.rollouts[key]; ok {
			return rollouts, nil
		}
	}
	return []*flipt.EvaluationRollout{}, nil
}

// mockFlagStore is a simple mock implementation for testing
type mockFlagStore struct {
	flags    map[string]*flipt.Flag
	rollouts map[string][]*storage.EvaluationRollout
}

func newMockFlagStore() *mockFlagStore {
	return &mockFlagStore{
		flags:    make(map[string]*flipt.Flag),
		rollouts: make(map[string][]*storage.EvaluationRollout),
	}
}

func (m *mockFlagStore) String() string {
	return "mock"
}

func (m *mockFlagStore) GetFlag(ctx context.Context, req storage.ResourceRequest) (*flipt.Flag, error) {
	// Create a key from namespace and flag key
	key := req.NamespaceKey + ":" + req.Key
	if flag, ok := m.flags[key]; ok {
		return flag, nil
	}
	return nil, fmt.Errorf("%s not found", req.Key)
}

func (m *mockFlagStore) GetEvaluationRules(ctx context.Context, req storage.ResourceRequest) ([]*storage.EvaluationRule, error) {
	return nil, nil
}

func (m *mockFlagStore) GetEvaluationDistributions(ctx context.Context, req storage.IDRequest) ([]*storage.EvaluationDistribution, error) {
	return nil, nil
}

func (m *mockFlagStore) GetEvaluationRollouts(ctx context.Context, req storage.ResourceRequest) ([]*storage.EvaluationRollout, error) {
	// Create a key from namespace and flag key
	key := req.NamespaceKey + ":" + req.Key
	if rollouts, ok := m.rollouts[key]; ok {
		return rollouts, nil
	}
	return []*storage.EvaluationRollout{}, nil
}

8. EDIT /workspace/integration/evaluation_integration_test.go
Before
	var result map[string]interface{}
	err = json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&result)
	require.NoError(t, err)

	// Check that flag_key exists in the response
	flagKey, ok := result["flag_key"]
	if !ok {
		// If flag_key is not at top level, check the structure

		t.Fatalf("expected flag_key in response, got %v", result)

	require.NoError(t, err)

	if result["flagKey"] != "feature_variant" {
		t.Fatalf("expected flagKey=feature_variant, got %v", result["flagKey"])
	}
